\hypertarget{raygui_8h_source}{}\doxysection{raygui.\+h}
\label{raygui_8h_source}\index{build/\_deps/raylib-\/src/examples/shapes/raygui.h@{build/\_deps/raylib-\/src/examples/shapes/raygui.h}}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{1 \textcolor{comment}{/*******************************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3 \textcolor{comment}{*   raygui v3.2 -\/ A simple and easy-\/to-\/use immediate-\/mode gui library}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5 \textcolor{comment}{*   DESCRIPTION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7 \textcolor{comment}{*   raygui is a tools-\/dev-\/focused immediate-\/mode-\/gui library based on raylib but also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8 \textcolor{comment}{*   available as a standalone library, as long as input and drawing functions are provided.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{9 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{10 \textcolor{comment}{*   Controls provided:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{11 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{12 \textcolor{comment}{*   \# Container/separators Controls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{13 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ WindowBox     -\/-\/> StatusBar, Panel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{14 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ GroupBox      -\/-\/> Line}}
\DoxyCodeLine{15 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Line}}
\DoxyCodeLine{16 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Panel         -\/-\/> StatusBar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{17 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ ScrollPanel   -\/-\/> StatusBar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{18 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{19 \textcolor{comment}{*   \# Basic Controls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{20 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Label}}
\DoxyCodeLine{21 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Button}}
\DoxyCodeLine{22 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ LabelButton   -\/-\/> Label}}
\DoxyCodeLine{23 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Toggle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{24 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ ToggleGroup   -\/-\/> Toggle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{25 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ CheckBox}}
\DoxyCodeLine{26 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ ComboBox}}
\DoxyCodeLine{27 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ DropdownBox}}
\DoxyCodeLine{28 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ TextBox}}
\DoxyCodeLine{29 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ TextBoxMulti}}
\DoxyCodeLine{30 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ ValueBox      -\/-\/> TextBox}}
\DoxyCodeLine{31 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Spinner       -\/-\/> Button, ValueBox}}
\DoxyCodeLine{32 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Slider}}
\DoxyCodeLine{33 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ SliderBar     -\/-\/> Slider}}
\DoxyCodeLine{34 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ ProgressBar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{35 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ StatusBar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{36 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ DummyRec}}
\DoxyCodeLine{37 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Grid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{38 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{39 \textcolor{comment}{*   \# Advance Controls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{40 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ ListView}}
\DoxyCodeLine{41 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ ColorPicker   -\/-\/> ColorPanel, ColorBarHue}}
\DoxyCodeLine{42 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ MessageBox    -\/-\/> Window, Label, Button}}
\DoxyCodeLine{43 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ TextInputBox  -\/-\/> Window, Label, TextBox, Button}}
\DoxyCodeLine{44 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{45 \textcolor{comment}{*   It also provides a set of functions for styling the controls based on its properties (size, color).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{46 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{47 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{48 \textcolor{comment}{*   RAYGUI STYLE (guiStyle):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{49 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{50 \textcolor{comment}{*   raygui uses a global data array for all gui style properties (allocated on data segment by default),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{51 \textcolor{comment}{*   when a new style is loaded, it is loaded over the global style... but a default gui style could always be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{52 \textcolor{comment}{*   recovered with GuiLoadStyleDefault() function, that overwrites the current style to the default one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{53 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{54 \textcolor{comment}{*   The global style array size is fixed and depends on the number of controls and properties:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{55 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{56 \textcolor{comment}{*       static unsigned int guiStyle[RAYGUI\_MAX\_CONTROLS*(RAYGUI\_MAX\_PROPS\_BASE + RAYGUI\_MAX\_PROPS\_EXTENDED)];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{57 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{58 \textcolor{comment}{*   guiStyle size is by default: 16*(16 + 8) = 384*4 = 1536 bytes = 1.5 KB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{59 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{60 \textcolor{comment}{*   Note that the first set of BASE properties (by default guiStyle[0..15]) belong to the generic style}}
\DoxyCodeLine{61 \textcolor{comment}{*   used for all controls, when any of those base values is set, it is automatically populated to all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{62 \textcolor{comment}{*   controls, so, specific control values overwriting generic style should be set after base values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{63 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{64 \textcolor{comment}{*   After the first BASE set we have the EXTENDED properties (by default guiStyle[16..23]), those}}
\DoxyCodeLine{65 \textcolor{comment}{*   properties are actually common to all controls and can not be overwritten individually (like BASE ones)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{66 \textcolor{comment}{*   Some of those properties are: TEXT\_SIZE, TEXT\_SPACING, LINE\_COLOR, BACKGROUND\_COLOR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{67 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{68 \textcolor{comment}{*   Custom control properties can be defined using the EXTENDED properties for each independent control.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{69 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{70 \textcolor{comment}{*   TOOL: rGuiStyler is a visual tool to customize raygui style.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{71 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{72 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{73 \textcolor{comment}{*   RAYGUI ICONS (guiIcons):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{74 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{75 \textcolor{comment}{*   raygui could use a global array containing icons data (allocated on data segment by default),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{76 \textcolor{comment}{*   a custom icons set could be loaded over this array using GuiLoadIcons(), but loaded icons set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{77 \textcolor{comment}{*   must be same RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE and no more than RAYGUI\_ICON\_MAX\_ICONS will be loaded}}
\DoxyCodeLine{78 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{79 \textcolor{comment}{*   Every icon is codified in binary form, using 1 bit per pixel, so, every 16x16 icon}}
\DoxyCodeLine{80 \textcolor{comment}{*   requires 8 integers (16*16/32) to be stored in memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{81 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{82 \textcolor{comment}{*   When the icon is draw, actually one quad per pixel is drawn if the bit for that pixel is set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{83 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{84 \textcolor{comment}{*   The global icons array size is fixed and depends on the number of icons and size:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{85 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{86 \textcolor{comment}{*       static unsigned int guiIcons[RAYGUI\_ICON\_MAX\_ICONS*RAYGUI\_ICON\_DATA\_ELEMENTS];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{87 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{88 \textcolor{comment}{*   guiIcons size is by default: 256*(16*16/32) = 2048*4 = 8192 bytes = 8 KB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{89 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{90 \textcolor{comment}{*   TOOL: rGuiIcons is a visual tool to customize raygui icons.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{91 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{92 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{93 \textcolor{comment}{*   CONFIGURATION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{94 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{95 \textcolor{comment}{*   \#define RAYGUI\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{96 \textcolor{comment}{*       Generates the implementation of the library into the included file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{97 \textcolor{comment}{*       If not defined, the library is in header only mode and can be included in other headers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{98 \textcolor{comment}{*       or source files without problems. But only ONE file should hold the implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{99 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{100 \textcolor{comment}{*   \#define RAYGUI\_STANDALONE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{101 \textcolor{comment}{*       Avoid raylib.h header inclusion in this file. Data types defined on raylib are defined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{102 \textcolor{comment}{*       internally in the library and input management and drawing functions must be provided by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{103 \textcolor{comment}{*       the user (check library implementation for further details).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{104 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{105 \textcolor{comment}{*   \#define RAYGUI\_NO\_ICONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{106 \textcolor{comment}{*       Avoid including embedded ricons data (256 icons, 16x16 pixels, 1-\/bit per pixel, 2KB)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{107 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{108 \textcolor{comment}{*   \#define RAYGUI\_CUSTOM\_ICONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{109 \textcolor{comment}{*       Includes custom ricons.h header defining a set of custom icons,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{110 \textcolor{comment}{*       this file can be generated using rGuiIcons tool}}
\DoxyCodeLine{111 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{112 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{113 \textcolor{comment}{*   VERSIONS HISTORY:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{204 }
\DoxyCodeLine{205 \textcolor{comment}{// Function specifiers in case library is build/used as a shared library (Windows)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{206 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Microsoft specifiers to tell compiler that symbols are imported/exported from a .dll}}
\DoxyCodeLine{207 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(\_WIN32)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{208 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#if defined(BUILD\_LIBTYPE\_SHARED)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{209 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#define RAYGUIAPI \_\_declspec(dllexport)     }\textcolor{comment}{// We are building the library as a Win32 shared library (.dll)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{210 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#elif defined(USE\_LIBTYPE\_SHARED)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{211 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#define RAYGUIAPI \_\_declspec(dllimport)     }\textcolor{comment}{// We are using the library as a Win32 shared library (.dll)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{212 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{213 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{214 }
\DoxyCodeLine{215 \textcolor{comment}{// Function specifiers definition}}

\DoxyCodeLine{217 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#define RAYGUIAPI       }\textcolor{comment}{// Functions defined as 'extern' by default (implicit specifiers)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{218 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{219 }

\DoxyCodeLine{234 \textcolor{comment}{// Simple log system to avoid printf() calls if required}}
\DoxyCodeLine{235 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Avoiding those calls, also avoids const strings memory usage}}
\DoxyCodeLine{236 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define RAYGUI\_SUPPORT\_LOG\_INFO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{237 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(RAYGUI\_SUPPORT\_LOG\_INFO)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{242 }
\DoxyCodeLine{243 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{244 \textcolor{comment}{// Types and Structures Definition}}
\DoxyCodeLine{245 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Some types are required for RAYGUI\_STANDALONE usage}}
\DoxyCodeLine{246 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{247 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(RAYGUI\_STANDALONE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{248 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#ifndef \_\_cplusplus}}
\DoxyCodeLine{249     \textcolor{comment}{// Boolean type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{250 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#ifndef true}}
\DoxyCodeLine{251             \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{enum} \{ \textcolor{keyword}{false}, \textcolor{keyword}{true} \} bool;}
\DoxyCodeLine{252 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{253 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{254 }
\DoxyCodeLine{255     \textcolor{comment}{// Vector2 type}}
\DoxyCodeLine{256     \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{structVector2}{Vector2}} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{257         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{258         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{259     \} \mbox{\hyperlink{structVector2}{Vector2}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{260 }
\DoxyCodeLine{261     \textcolor{comment}{// Vector3 type                 // -\/-\/ ConvertHSVtoRGB(), ConvertRGBtoHSV()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{262     \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{structVector3}{Vector3}} \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{853 }
\DoxyCodeLine{854 \textcolor{comment}{// Embedded icons, no external file provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{855 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE               16          }\textcolor{comment}{// Size of icons in pixels (squared)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{856 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define RAYGUI\_ICON\_MAX\_ICONS         256          }\textcolor{comment}{// Maximum number of icons}}
\DoxyCodeLine{857 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define RAYGUI\_ICON\_MAX\_NAME\_LENGTH    32          }\textcolor{comment}{// Maximum length of icon name id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{858 }
\DoxyCodeLine{859 \textcolor{comment}{// Icons data is defined by bit array (every bit represents one pixel)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{860 \textcolor{comment}{// Those arrays are stored as unsigned int data arrays, so,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{861 \textcolor{comment}{// every array element defines 32 pixels (bits) of information}}
\DoxyCodeLine{862 \textcolor{comment}{// One icon is defined by 8 int, (8 int * 32 bit = 256 bit = 16*16 pixels)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{863 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Number of elemens depend on RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE (by default 16x16 pixels)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{864 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define RAYGUI\_ICON\_DATA\_ELEMENTS   (RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE*RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE/32)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{865 }
\DoxyCodeLine{866 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{867 \textcolor{comment}{// Icons data for all gui possible icons (allocated on data segment by default)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{868 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{869 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE 1: Every icon is codified in binary form, using 1 bit per pixel, so,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{870 \textcolor{comment}{// every 16x16 icon requires 8 integers (16*16/32) to be stored}}
\DoxyCodeLine{871 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{872 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE 2: A different icon set could be loaded over this array using GuiLoadIcons(),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{873 \textcolor{comment}{// but loaded icons set must be same RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE and no more than RAYGUI\_ICON\_MAX\_ICONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{874 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{875 \textcolor{comment}{// guiIcons size is by default: 256*(16*16/32) = 2048*4 = 8192 bytes = 8 KB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{876 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1168 \textcolor{comment}{// can not be overwritten individually but custom EXTENDED properties can be used by control}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1169 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1170 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE 2: A new style set could be loaded over this array using GuiLoadStyle(),}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1172 \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1728 \textcolor{comment}{// Toggle Group control, returns toggled button index}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1729 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} GuiToggleGroup(\mbox{\hyperlink{structRectangle}{Rectangle}} bounds, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *text, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} active)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1730 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1731 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#if !defined(RAYGUI\_TOGGLEGROUP\_MAX\_ITEMS)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1732 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#define RAYGUI\_TOGGLEGROUP\_MAX\_ITEMS    32}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1733 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1734 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1735     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} initBoundsX = bounds.x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1736 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1737     \textcolor{comment}{// Get substrings items from text (items pointers)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1738     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} rows[RAYGUI\_TOGGLEGROUP\_MAX\_ITEMS] = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1739     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} itemCount = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1740     \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} **items = GuiTextSplit(text, \&itemCount, rows);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1741 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1742     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} prevRow = rows[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1743 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1744     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; i < itemCount; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1745     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1746         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (prevRow != rows[i])}
\DoxyCodeLine{1747         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1748             bounds.x = initBoundsX;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1749             bounds.y += (bounds.height + GuiGetStyle(TOGGLE, GROUP\_PADDING));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1750             prevRow = rows[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1751         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1752 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1753         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (i == active) GuiToggle(bounds, items[i], \textcolor{keyword}{true});}
\DoxyCodeLine{1754         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (GuiToggle(bounds, items[i], \textcolor{keyword}{false}) == \textcolor{keyword}{true}) active = i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1755 }

\DoxyCodeLine{2455 \textcolor{comment}{// Slider control with pro parameters}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2457 \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} GuiSliderPro(\mbox{\hyperlink{structRectangle}{Rectangle}} bounds, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *textLeft, \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *textRight, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} value, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} minValue, \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} maxValue, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} sliderWidth)}

\DoxyCodeLine{2477     \textcolor{comment}{// Update control}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2496         \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2507     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2687     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((startIndex < 0) || (startIndex > (count -\/ visibleItems))) startIndex = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2688     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} endIndex = startIndex + visibleItems;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2689 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2690     \textcolor{comment}{// Update control}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2691     \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2703             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2704                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (CheckCollisionPointRec(mousePoint, itemBounds))}
\DoxyCodeLine{2705                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{2706                     itemFocused = startIndex + i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2707                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (IsMouseButtonPressed(MOUSE\_LEFT\_BUTTON))}
\DoxyCodeLine{2708                     \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{2710                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} itemSelected = startIndex + i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2711                     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2712                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{2713                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2714 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2715                 \textcolor{comment}{// Update item rectangle y position for next item}}

\DoxyCodeLine{2717             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2718 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2719             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (useScrollBar)}

\DoxyCodeLine{2723 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2724                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (startIndex < 0) startIndex = 0;}

\DoxyCodeLine{2726 }
\DoxyCodeLine{2727                 endIndex = startIndex + visibleItems;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2728                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (endIndex > count) endIndex = count;}
\DoxyCodeLine{2729             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2730         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2731         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} itemFocused = -\/1;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3250 \textcolor{comment}{// Load raygui style file (.rgs)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3251 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: By default a binary file is expected, that file could contain a custom font,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3252 \textcolor{comment}{// in that case, custom font image atlas is GRAY+ALPHA and pixel data can be compressed (DEFLATE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3253 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} GuiLoadStyle(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *fileName)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3254 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3255 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#define MAX\_LINE\_BUFFER\_SIZE    256}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3256 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3257     \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} tryBinary = \textcolor{keyword}{false};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3258 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3259     \textcolor{comment}{// Try reading the files as text file first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3260     FILE *rgsFile = fopen(fileName, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}rt"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{3261 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3262     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rgsFile != NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3263     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3264         \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} buffer[MAX\_LINE\_BUFFER\_SIZE] = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3265         fgets(buffer, MAX\_LINE\_BUFFER\_SIZE, rgsFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3266 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3267         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (buffer[0] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\#'})}
\DoxyCodeLine{3268         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3269             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} controlId = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3270             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} propertyId = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3271             \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} propertyValue = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3272 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3273             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (!feof(rgsFile))}
\DoxyCodeLine{3274             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3275                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (buffer[0])}
\DoxyCodeLine{3276                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3277                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'p'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3278                     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3279                         \textcolor{comment}{// Style property: p <control\_id> <property\_id> <property\_value> <property\_name>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3280 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3281                         sscanf(buffer, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}p \%d \%d 0x\%x"{}}, \&controlId, \&propertyId, \&propertyValue);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3282                         GuiSetStyle(controlId, propertyId, (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})propertyValue);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3283 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3284                     \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3285                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \textcolor{charliteral}{'f'}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{3286                     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3287                         \textcolor{comment}{// Style font: f <gen\_font\_size> <charmap\_file> <font\_file>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3288 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3289                         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} fontSize = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3290                         \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} charmapFileName[256] = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3291                         \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} fontFileName[256] = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3292                         sscanf(buffer, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}f \%d \%s \%[\string^\(\backslash\)r\(\backslash\)n]s"{}}, \&fontSize, charmapFileName, fontFileName);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3293 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3294                         \mbox{\hyperlink{structFont}{Font}} font = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3295 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3296                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (charmapFileName[0] != \textcolor{charliteral}{'0'})}
\DoxyCodeLine{3297                         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3298                             \textcolor{comment}{// Load characters from charmap file,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3299                             \textcolor{comment}{// expected '\(\backslash\)n' separated list of integer values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3300                             \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *charValues = LoadFileText(charmapFileName);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3301                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (charValues != NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3302                             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3303                                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} glyphCount = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3304                                 \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} **chars = TextSplit(charValues, \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)n'}, \&glyphCount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3305 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3306                                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *values = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *)RAYGUI\_MALLOC(glyphCount*\textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}));}
\DoxyCodeLine{3307                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; i < glyphCount; i++) values[i] = TextToInteger(chars[i]);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3308 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3309                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (font.texture.id != GetFontDefault().texture.id) UnloadTexture(font.texture);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3310                                 font = LoadFontEx(TextFormat(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\%s/\%s"{}}, GetDirectoryPath(fileName), fontFileName), fontSize, values, glyphCount);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3311                                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (font.texture.id == 0) font = GetFontDefault();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3312 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3313                                 RAYGUI\_FREE(values);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3314                             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3315                         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3316                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3317                         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3318                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (font.texture.id != GetFontDefault().texture.id) UnloadTexture(font.texture);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3319                             font = LoadFontEx(TextFormat(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\%s/\%s"{}}, GetDirectoryPath(fileName), fontFileName), fontSize, NULL, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3320                             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (font.texture.id == 0) font = GetFontDefault();}
\DoxyCodeLine{3321                         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3322 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3323                         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((font.texture.id > 0) \&\& (font.glyphCount > 0)) GuiSetFont(font);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3324 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3325                     \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3326                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3327                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3328 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3329                 fgets(buffer, MAX\_LINE\_BUFFER\_SIZE, rgsFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3330             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3331         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3332         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} tryBinary = \textcolor{keyword}{true};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3333 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3334         fclose(rgsFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3335     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3336 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3337     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tryBinary)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3338     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3339         rgsFile = fopen(fileName, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}rb"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{3340 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3341         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rgsFile == NULL) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3342 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3343         \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} signature[5] = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3344         \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} version = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3345         \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} reserved = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3346         \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} propertyCount = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3347 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3348         fread(signature, 1, 4, rgsFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3349         fread(\&version, 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}), rgsFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3350         fread(\&reserved, 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}), rgsFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3351         fread(\&propertyCount, 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}), rgsFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3352 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3353         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((signature[0] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'r'}) \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{3354             (signature[1] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'G'}) \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{3355             (signature[2] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'S'}) \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{3356             (signature[3] == \textcolor{charliteral}{' '}))}
\DoxyCodeLine{3357         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3358             \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} controlId = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3359             \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} propertyId = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3360             \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} propertyValue = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3361 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3362             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; i < propertyCount; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3363             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3364                 fread(\&controlId, 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}), rgsFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3365                 fread(\&propertyId, 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}), rgsFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3366                 fread(\&propertyValue, 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}), rgsFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3367 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3368                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (controlId == 0) \textcolor{comment}{// DEFAULT control}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3369                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3370                     \textcolor{comment}{// If a DEFAULT property is loaded, it is propagated to all controls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3371                     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: All DEFAULT properties should be defined first in the file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3372                     GuiSetStyle(0, (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})propertyId, propertyValue);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3373 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3374                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (propertyId < RAYGUI\_MAX\_PROPS\_BASE) \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 1; i < RAYGUI\_MAX\_CONTROLS; i++) GuiSetStyle(i, (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})propertyId, propertyValue);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3375                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3376                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} GuiSetStyle((\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})controlId, (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})propertyId, propertyValue);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3377             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3378 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3379             \textcolor{comment}{// Font loading is highly dependant on raylib API to load font data and image}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3382             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} fontDataSize = 0;}

\DoxyCodeLine{3385             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (fontDataSize > 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3386             \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{3394 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3395                 \textcolor{comment}{// Load font white rectangle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3396                 fread(\&whiteRec, 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\mbox{\hyperlink{structRectangle}{Rectangle}}), rgsFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3397 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3398                 \textcolor{comment}{// Load font image parameters}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3399                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} fontImageUncompSize = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3400                 \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} fontImageCompSize = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3401                 fread(\&fontImageUncompSize, 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}), rgsFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3402                 fread(\&fontImageCompSize, 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}), rgsFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3403 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3404                 \mbox{\hyperlink{structImage}{Image}} imFont = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3405                 imFont.mipmaps = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3406                 fread(\&imFont.width, 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}), rgsFile);}

\DoxyCodeLine{3410                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (fontImageCompSize < fontImageUncompSize)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3411                 \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{3413                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} dataUncompSize = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3414                     \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *compData = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *)RAYGUI\_MALLOC(fontImageCompSize);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3415                     fread(compData, 1, fontImageCompSize, rgsFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3416                     imFont.data = DecompressData(compData, fontImageCompSize, \&dataUncompSize);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3417 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3418                     \textcolor{comment}{// Security check, dataUncompSize must match the provided fontImageUncompSize}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3419                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (dataUncompSize != fontImageUncompSize) RAYGUI\_LOG(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}WARNING: Uncompressed font atlas image data could be corrupted"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{3420 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3421                     RAYGUI\_FREE(compData);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3422                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3423                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3424                 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3425                     \textcolor{comment}{// Font atlas image data is not compressed}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3580 \textcolor{comment}{// Load raygui icons file (.rgi)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3581 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: In case nameIds are required, they can be requested with loadIconsName,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3585 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3586     \textcolor{comment}{// Style File Structure (.rgi)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3587     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3588     \textcolor{comment}{// Offset  | Size    | Type       | Description}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3589     \textcolor{comment}{// -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3590     \textcolor{comment}{// 0       | 4       | char       | Signature: "{}rGI "{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3591     \textcolor{comment}{// 4       | 2       | short      | Version: 100}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3592     \textcolor{comment}{// 6       | 2       | short      | reserved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3593 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3594     \textcolor{comment}{// 8       | 2       | short      | Num icons (N)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3595     \textcolor{comment}{// 10      | 2       | short      | Icons size (Options: 16, 32, 64) (S)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3596 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3597     \textcolor{comment}{// Icons name id (32 bytes per name id)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3598     \textcolor{comment}{// foreach (icon)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3599     \textcolor{comment}{// \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3600     \textcolor{comment}{//   12+32*i  | 32   | char       | Icon NameId}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3601     \textcolor{comment}{// \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3602 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3603     \textcolor{comment}{// Icons data: One bit per pixel, stored as unsigned int array (depends on icon size)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3604     \textcolor{comment}{// S*S pixels/32bit per unsigned int = K unsigned int per icon}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3605     \textcolor{comment}{// foreach (icon)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3606     \textcolor{comment}{// \{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3607     \textcolor{comment}{//   ...   | K       | unsigned int | Icon Data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3608     \textcolor{comment}{// \}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3609 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3610     FILE *rgiFile = fopen(fileName, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}rb"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{3611 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3612     \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} **guiIconsName = NULL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3613 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3614     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rgiFile != NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3615     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3616         \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} signature[5] = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3617         \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} version = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3618         \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} reserved = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3619         \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} iconCount = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3620         \textcolor{keywordtype}{short} iconSize = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3621 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3622         fread(signature, 1, 4, rgiFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3623         fread(\&version, 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}), rgiFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3624         fread(\&reserved, 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}), rgiFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3625         fread(\&iconCount, 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}), rgiFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3626         fread(\&iconSize, 1, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{short}), rgiFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3627 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3628         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((signature[0] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'r'}) \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{3629             (signature[1] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'G'}) \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{3630             (signature[2] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'I'}) \&\&}
\DoxyCodeLine{3631             (signature[3] == \textcolor{charliteral}{' '}))}
\DoxyCodeLine{3632         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3633             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (loadIconsName)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3634             \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{3640                 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3641             \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3643 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3644             \textcolor{comment}{// Read icons data directly over guiIcons data array}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3646         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3647 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3648         fclose(rgiFile);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3649     \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3654 \textcolor{comment}{// Draw selected icon using rectangles pixel-\/by-\/pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3655 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} GuiDrawIcon(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} iconId, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} posX, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} posY, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pixelSize, \mbox{\hyperlink{structColor}{Color}} color)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3656 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3657 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#define BIT\_CHECK(a,b) ((a) \& (1u<<(b)))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3658 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3659     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0, y = 0; i < RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE*RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE/32; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3660     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3661         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} k = 0; k < 32; k++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3662         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3663             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (BIT\_CHECK(guiIcons[iconId*RAYGUI\_ICON\_DATA\_ELEMENTS + i], k))}
\DoxyCodeLine{3664             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3665 \textcolor{preprocessor}{            \#if !defined(RAYGUI\_STANDALONE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3666                 DrawRectangle(posX + (k\%RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE)*pixelSize, posY + y*pixelSize, pixelSize, pixelSize, color);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3667 \textcolor{preprocessor}{            \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3668             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3669 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3670             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((k == 15) || (k == 31)) y++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3671         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3672     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3673 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3700 \textcolor{comment}{// Set icon pixel value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3701 \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} GuiSetIconPixel(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} iconId, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} x, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} y)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3702 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3703 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#define BIT\_SET(a,b)   ((a) |= (1u<<(b)))}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3704 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3705     \textcolor{comment}{// This logic works for any RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE pixels icons,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3706     \textcolor{comment}{// For example, in case of 16x16 pixels, every 2 lines fit in one unsigned int data element}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3919 \textcolor{comment}{// Split controls text into multiple strings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3920 \textcolor{comment}{// Also check for multiple columns (required by GuiToggleGroup())}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3921 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} **GuiTextSplit(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *text, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *textRow)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3922 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3923     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Current implementation returns a copy of the provided string with '\(\backslash\)0' (string end delimiter)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3924     \textcolor{comment}{// inserted between strings defined by "{}delimiter"{} parameter. No memory is dynamically allocated,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3925     \textcolor{comment}{// all used memory is static... it has some limitations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3926     \textcolor{comment}{//      1. Maximum number of possible split strings is set by RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3927     \textcolor{comment}{//      2. Maximum size of text to split is RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3928     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Those definitions could be externally provided if required}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3929 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3930 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#if !defined(RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3931 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#define RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS        128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3932 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3933 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#if !defined(RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3934 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#define RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE      1024}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3935 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3936 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3937     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *result[RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS] = \{ NULL \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3938     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} buffer[RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE] = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3939     memset(buffer, 0, RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3940 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3941     result[0] = buffer;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3942     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} counter = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3943 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3944     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (textRow != NULL) textRow[0] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3945 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3946     \textcolor{comment}{// Count how many substrings we have on text and point to every one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3947     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; i < RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3948     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3949         buffer[i] = text[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3950         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (buffer[i] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3951         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((buffer[i] == \textcolor{charliteral}{';'}) || (buffer[i] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)n'}))}
\DoxyCodeLine{3952         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3953             result[counter] = buffer + i + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3954 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3955             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (textRow != NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3956             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3957                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (buffer[i] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)n'}) textRow[counter] = textRow[counter -\/ 1] + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3958                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} textRow[counter] = textRow[counter -\/ 1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3959             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3960 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3961             buffer[i] = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'};   \textcolor{comment}{// Set an end of string at this point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3962 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3963             counter++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3964             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (counter == RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3965         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3966     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3967 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3968     *count = counter;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3969 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3970     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3971 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3972 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3973 \textcolor{comment}{// Convert color data from RGB to HSV}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3974 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Color data should be passed normalized}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3975 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \mbox{\hyperlink{structVector3}{Vector3}} ConvertRGBtoHSV(\mbox{\hyperlink{structVector3}{Vector3}} rgb)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3976 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3977     \mbox{\hyperlink{structVector3}{Vector3}} hsv = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3978     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} min = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3979     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} max = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3980     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} delta = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3981 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3982     min = (rgb.x < rgb.y)? rgb.x : rgb.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3983     min = (min < rgb.z)? min  : rgb.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3984 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3985     max = (rgb.x > rgb.y)? rgb.x : rgb.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3986     max = (max > rgb.z)? max  : rgb.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3987 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3988     hsv.z = max;            \textcolor{comment}{// Value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3989     delta = max -\/ min;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3990 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3991     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (delta < 0.00001f)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3992     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3993         hsv.y = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3994         hsv.x = 0.0f;           \textcolor{comment}{// Undefined, maybe NAN?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3995         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} hsv;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3996     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3997 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3998     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (max > 0.0f)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3999     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4000         \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: If max is 0, this divide would cause a crash}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4001         hsv.y = (delta/max);    \textcolor{comment}{// Saturation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4002     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4003     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4004     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4005         \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: If max is 0, then r = g = b = 0, s = 0, h is undefined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4006         hsv.y = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4007         hsv.x = 0.0f;           \textcolor{comment}{// Undefined, maybe NAN?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4008         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} hsv;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4009     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4010 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4011     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Comparing float values could not work properly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4012     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rgb.x >= max) hsv.x = (rgb.y -\/ rgb.z)/delta;    \textcolor{comment}{// Between yellow \& magenta}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4013     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4014     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4015         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rgb.y >= max) hsv.x = 2.0f + (rgb.z -\/ rgb.x)/delta;  \textcolor{comment}{// Between cyan \& yellow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4016         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} hsv.x = 4.0f + (rgb.x -\/ rgb.y)/delta;      \textcolor{comment}{// Between magenta \& cyan}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4017     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4018 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4019     hsv.x *= 60.0f;     \textcolor{comment}{// Convert to degrees}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4020 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4021     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (hsv.x < 0.0f) hsv.x += 360.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4022 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4023     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} hsv;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4024 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4025 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4026 \textcolor{comment}{// Convert color data from HSV to RGB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4027 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Color data should be passed normalized}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4028 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \mbox{\hyperlink{structVector3}{Vector3}} ConvertHSVtoRGB(\mbox{\hyperlink{structVector3}{Vector3}} hsv)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4029 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4030     \mbox{\hyperlink{structVector3}{Vector3}} rgb = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4031     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} hh = 0.0f, p = 0.0f, q = 0.0f, t = 0.0f, ff = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4032     \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} i = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4033 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4034     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Comparing float values could not work properly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4035     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (hsv.y <= 0.0f)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4036     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4037         rgb.x = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4038         rgb.y = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4039         rgb.z = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4040         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} rgb;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4041     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4042 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4043     hh = hsv.x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4044     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (hh >= 360.0f) hh = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4045     hh /= 60.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4046 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4047     i = (long)hh;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4048     ff = hh -\/ i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4049     p = hsv.z*(1.0f -\/ hsv.y);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4050     q = hsv.z*(1.0f -\/ (hsv.y*ff));}
\DoxyCodeLine{4051     t = hsv.z*(1.0f -\/ (hsv.y*(1.0f -\/ ff)));}
\DoxyCodeLine{4052 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4053     \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4054     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4055         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 0:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4056         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4057             rgb.x = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4058             rgb.y = t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4059             rgb.z = p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4060         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4061         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 1:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4062         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4063             rgb.x = q;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4064             rgb.y = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4065             rgb.z = p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4066         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4067         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 2:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4068         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4069             rgb.x = p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4070             rgb.y = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4071             rgb.z = t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4072         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4073         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 3:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4074         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4075             rgb.x = p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4076             rgb.y = q;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4077             rgb.z = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4078         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4079         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 4:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4080         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4081             rgb.x = t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4082             rgb.y = p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4083             rgb.z = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4084         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4085         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 5:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4086         \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4087         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4088             rgb.x = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4089             rgb.y = p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4090             rgb.z = q;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4091         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4092     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4093 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4094     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} rgb;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4095 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4096 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4279 \textcolor{comment}{// Split string into multiple strings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4280 \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} **TextSplit(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *text, \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} delimiter, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *count)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4281 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4282     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Current implementation returns a copy of the provided string with '\(\backslash\)0' (string end delimiter)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4283     \textcolor{comment}{// inserted between strings defined by "{}delimiter"{} parameter. No memory is dynamically allocated,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4284     \textcolor{comment}{// all used memory is static... it has some limitations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4285     \textcolor{comment}{//      1. Maximum number of possible split strings is set by RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4286     \textcolor{comment}{//      2. Maximum size of text to split is RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4287 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4288 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#if !defined(RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4289 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#define RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS        128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4290 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4291 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#if !defined(RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4292 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#define RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE      1024}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4293 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4294 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4295     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *result[RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS] = \{ NULL \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4296     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} buffer[RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE] = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4297     memset(buffer, 0, RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4298 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4299     result[0] = buffer;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4300     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} counter = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4301 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4302     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (text != NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4303     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4304         counter = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4305 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4306         \textcolor{comment}{// Count how many substrings we have on text and point to every one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4307         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; i < RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4308         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4309             buffer[i] = text[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4310             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (buffer[i] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4311             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (buffer[i] == delimiter)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4312             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4313                 buffer[i] = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'};   \textcolor{comment}{// Set an end of string at this point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4314                 result[counter] = buffer + i + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4315                 counter++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4316 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4317                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (counter == RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4318             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4319         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4320     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4321 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4322     *count = counter;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4323     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4324 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4325 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4326 \textcolor{comment}{// Get integer value from text}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4327 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: This function replaces atoi() [stdlib.h]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4328 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} TextToInteger(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *text)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4329 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4330     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} value = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4331     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} sign = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4332 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4333     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((text[0] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'+'}) || (text[0] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'-\/'}))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4334     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4335         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (text[0] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'-\/'}) sign = -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4336         text++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4337     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4338 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4339     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; ((text[i] >= \textcolor{charliteral}{'0'}) \&\& (text[i] <= \textcolor{charliteral}{'9'})); ++i) value = value*10 + (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})(text[i] -\/ \textcolor{charliteral}{'0'});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4340 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4341     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} value*sign;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4342 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4343 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4344 \textcolor{comment}{// Encode codepoint into UTF-\/8 text (char array size returned as parameter)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4345 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *CodepointToUTF8(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} codepoint, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *byteSize)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4346 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4347     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} utf8[6] = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4348     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} size = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4349 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4350     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (codepoint <= 0x7f)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4351     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4352         utf8[0] = (char)codepoint;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4353         size = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4354     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4355     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (codepoint <= 0x7ff)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4356     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4357         utf8[0] = (char)(((codepoint >> 6) \& 0x1f) | 0xc0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4358         utf8[1] = (char)((codepoint \& 0x3f) | 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4359         size = 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4360     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4361     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (codepoint <= 0xffff)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4362     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4363         utf8[0] = (char)(((codepoint >> 12) \& 0x0f) | 0xe0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4364         utf8[1] = (char)(((codepoint >>  6) \& 0x3f) | 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4365         utf8[2] = (char)((codepoint \& 0x3f) | 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4366         size = 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4367     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4368     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (codepoint <= 0x10ffff)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4369     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4370         utf8[0] = (char)(((codepoint >> 18) \& 0x07) | 0xf0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4371         utf8[1] = (char)(((codepoint >> 12) \& 0x3f) | 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4372         utf8[2] = (char)(((codepoint >>  6) \& 0x3f) | 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4373         utf8[3] = (char)((codepoint \& 0x3f) | 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4374         size = 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4375     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4376 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4377     *byteSize = size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4378 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4379     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} utf8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4380 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4381 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4382 \textcolor{comment}{// Get next codepoint in a UTF-\/8 encoded text, scanning until '\(\backslash\)0' is found}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4383 \textcolor{comment}{// When a invalid UTF-\/8 byte is encountered we exit as soon as possible and a '?'(0x3f) codepoint is returned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4384 \textcolor{comment}{// Total number of bytes processed are returned as a parameter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4385 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: the standard says U+FFFD should be returned in case of errors}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4386 \textcolor{comment}{// but that character is not supported by the default font in raylib}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4387 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} GetCodepoint(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *text, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *bytesProcessed)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4388 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4389 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4390 \textcolor{comment}{    UTF-\/8 specs from https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc3629.txt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4391 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4392 \textcolor{comment}{    Char. number range  |        UTF-\/8 octet sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4393 \textcolor{comment}{      (hexadecimal)    |              (binary)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4394 \textcolor{comment}{    -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4395 \textcolor{comment}{    0000 0000-\/0000 007F | 0xxxxxxx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4396 \textcolor{comment}{    0000 0080-\/0000 07FF | 110xxxxx 10xxxxxx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4397 \textcolor{comment}{    0000 0800-\/0000 FFFF | 1110xxxx 10xxxxxx 10xxxxxx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4398 \textcolor{comment}{    0001 0000-\/0010 FFFF | 11110xxx 10xxxxxx 10xxxxxx 10xxxxxx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4399 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4400     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: on decode errors we return as soon as possible}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4401 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4402     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} code = 0x3f;   \textcolor{comment}{// Codepoint (defaults to '?')}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4403     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} octet = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(text[0]); \textcolor{comment}{// The first UTF8 octet}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4404     *bytesProcessed = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4405 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4406     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (octet <= 0x7f)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4407     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4408         \textcolor{comment}{// Only one octet (ASCII range x00-\/7F)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4409         code = text[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4410     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4411     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet \& 0xe0) == 0xc0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4412     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4413         \textcolor{comment}{// Two octets}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4414 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4415         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xC2-\/DF    [1]UTF8-\/tail(x80-\/BF)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4416         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} octet1 = text[1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4417 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4418         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet1 == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) || ((octet1 >> 6) != 2)) \{ *bytesProcessed = 2; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \} \textcolor{comment}{// Unexpected sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4419 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4420         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet >= 0xc2) \&\& (octet <= 0xdf))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4421         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4422             code = ((octet \& 0x1f) << 6) | (octet1 \& 0x3f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4423             *bytesProcessed = 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4424         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4425     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4426     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet \& 0xf0) == 0xe0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4427     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4428         \textcolor{comment}{// Three octets}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4429         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} octet1 = text[1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4430         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} octet2 = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4431 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4432         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet1 == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) || ((octet1 >> 6) != 2)) \{ *bytesProcessed = 2; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \} \textcolor{comment}{// Unexpected sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4433 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4434         octet2 = text[2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4435 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4436         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet2 == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) || ((octet2 >> 6) != 2)) \{ *bytesProcessed = 3; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \} \textcolor{comment}{// Unexpected sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4437 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4438         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xE0    [1]xA0-\/BF       [2]UTF8-\/tail(x80-\/BF)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4439         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xE1-\/EC [1]UTF8-\/tail    [2]UTF8-\/tail(x80-\/BF)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4440         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xED    [1]x80-\/9F       [2]UTF8-\/tail(x80-\/BF)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4441         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xEE-\/EF [1]UTF8-\/tail    [2]UTF8-\/tail(x80-\/BF)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4442 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4443         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (((octet == 0xe0) \&\& !((octet1 >= 0xa0) \&\& (octet1 <= 0xbf))) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{4444             ((octet == 0xed) \&\& !((octet1 >= 0x80) \&\& (octet1 <= 0x9f)))) \{ *bytesProcessed = 2; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4445 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4446         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet >= 0xe0) \&\& (0 <= 0xef))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4447         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4448             code = ((octet \& 0xf) << 12) | ((octet1 \& 0x3f) << 6) | (octet2 \& 0x3f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4449             *bytesProcessed = 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4450         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4451     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4452     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet \& 0xf8) == 0xf0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4453     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4454         \textcolor{comment}{// Four octets}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4455         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (octet > 0xf4) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4456 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4457         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} octet1 = text[1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4458         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} octet2 = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4459         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} octet3 = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4460 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4461         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet1 == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) || ((octet1 >> 6) != 2)) \{ *bytesProcessed = 2; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \}  \textcolor{comment}{// Unexpected sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4462 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4463         octet2 = text[2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4464 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4465         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet2 == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) || ((octet2 >> 6) != 2)) \{ *bytesProcessed = 3; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \}  \textcolor{comment}{// Unexpected sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4466 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4467         octet3 = text[3];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4468 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4469         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet3 == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) || ((octet3 >> 6) != 2)) \{ *bytesProcessed = 4; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \}  \textcolor{comment}{// Unexpected sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4470 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4471         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xF0       [1]x90-\/BF       [2]UTF8-\/tail  [3]UTF8-\/tail}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4472         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xF1-\/F3    [1]UTF8-\/tail    [2]UTF8-\/tail  [3]UTF8-\/tail}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4473         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xF4       [1]x80-\/8F       [2]UTF8-\/tail  [3]UTF8-\/tail}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4474 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4475         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (((octet == 0xf0) \&\& !((octet1 >= 0x90) \&\& (octet1 <= 0xbf))) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{4476             ((octet == 0xf4) \&\& !((octet1 >= 0x80) \&\& (octet1 <= 0x8f)))) \{ *bytesProcessed = 2; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \} \textcolor{comment}{// Unexpected sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4477 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4478         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (octet >= 0xf0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4479         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4480             code = ((octet \& 0x7) << 18) | ((octet1 \& 0x3f) << 12) | ((octet2 \& 0x3f) << 6) | (octet3 \& 0x3f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4481             *bytesProcessed = 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4482         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4483     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4484 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4485     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code > 0x10ffff) code = 0x3f;     \textcolor{comment}{// Codepoints after U+10ffff are invalid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4486 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4487     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4488 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4489 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif      }\textcolor{comment}{// RAYGUI\_STANDALONE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4490 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4491 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif      }\textcolor{comment}{// RAYGUI\_IMPLEMENTATION}}

\end{DoxyCode}
